name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

Please make Mac and MS name table entries the same OR remove all Mac entries (new, Nov. 2020).
Further read: App test: no Mac name table

Entries are different (English).
Mac [1, 0, 0] is: 'No entry.'
MS [3, 1, 1033] is: 'https://scripts.sil.org/OFL'

Warning

JetBrains Mono Regular (JetBrainsMono[wght].ttf)

name

Mac NID 0 (Mac/Roman/English)

Necessary name table entry according Monotype: 'Mac NID 0, Copyright' (Mac/Roman/English)

Copyright NID 0 (Mac/Roman/English) is missing.
Please verify agains spec. It might be ok if it's a symbol font.

name

MS NID 0 (3, 1, 1033, 0)

MS NID 0, Copyright.

Please verify agains spec.
MS NID 0 is 'Copyright 2020 The JetBrains Mono Project Authors (https://github.com/JetBrains/JetBrainsMono)'
It should follow this structure: 'Copyright (c) XXXX - XXXX /entity/. All rights reserved.'

JetBrains Mono Italic (JetBrainsMono-Italic[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'JetBrainsMono-Italic', Everything looks good.

Pass

JetBrains Mono Regular (JetBrainsMono[wght].ttf)

gasp

Default

Check gasp table Default.

gasp table default is:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
and should be:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
